                          <h3 class=\"HCard-title u-block u-textBold\">Three Series of Exclusive FlipTips Now Available at NewForce.tft.com</h3>\n                                <div class=\"HCard-imgBlock\">\n                                    <img class=\"HCard-img\" src=\"https://firerescue1-praetorian.netdna-ssl.com/whats-hot-images/TFT-WH-8-7.png\" alt=\"Three Series of Exclusive FlipTips Now Available at NewForce.tft.com\">\n                                </div>\n                        </a>\n                            <div class=\"HCard-textsWrap\">\n
